        const majorDetail = document.getElementById('majorDetail');
        const overlay = document.getElementById('overlay');
        const zoomControls = document.getElementById('zoomControls');
        
        let width, height, centerX, centerY;
        let currentView = 'spiral';
        let selectedYear = null;
        
        let rotationY = 0;
        let autoRotate = true;
        let isDragging = false;
        let lastTouchX = 0;
        
        let solarRotX = 0.5;
        let solarRotY = 0;
        let solarDragging = false;
        // 触控双击检测变量
        let lastTapTime = 0;
        let lastTapX = 0;
        let lastTapY = 0;
        const TAP_THRESHOLD = 30;  // 触控容错范围
        const DOUBLE_TAP_DELAY = 300;  // 双击间隔(ms)

        let solarLastX = 0;
        let solarLastY = 0;
        let zoomLevel = 1;
        
        // 动画相关
        let animationTime = 0;
        let majorRotationAngles = []; // 每个学院的专业旋转角度
        
        const startYear = 1956;
        const endYear = 2025;
        const totalYears = endYear - startYear + 1;
        const rings = 6;
        const spiralHeight = 800;
        
        let spiralNodes = [];
        let collegeNodes = [];
        
        function resize() {
            const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
            width = window.innerWidth;
            height = window.innerHeight;
            canvas.width = width * dpr;
            canvas.height = height * dpr;
            canvas.style.width = width + 'px';
            canvas.style.height = height + 'px';
            ctx.scale(dpr, dpr);
            centerX = width / 2;
            centerY = height / 2;
            generateSpiralNodes();
        }
        
        function generateSpiralNodes() {
            spiralNodes = [];
            const baseRadius = Math.min(width, height) * 0.18;
            for (let i = 0; i < totalYears; i++) {
                const year = startYear + i;
                const progress = i / totalYears;
                const angle = progress * rings * Math.PI * 2;
                spiralNodes.push({ 
                    localX: Math.cos(angle) * baseRadius,
                    localY: (1 - progress) * spiralHeight - spiralHeight / 2,
                    localZ: Math.sin(angle) * baseRadius,
                    x: 0, y: 0, scale: 1, 
                    year, count: getMajorCount(year), 
                    size: 12, // 统一大小
                    specialColor: (function() {
                        const specialYears = {
                            1956: '#FF6B6B', // 建校 - 红色
                            1958: '#FFA500', // 更名 - 橙色
                            1965: '#9370DB', // 迁入 - 紫色
                            1993: '#FFA500', // 更名 - 橙色
                            2001: '#FFD700', // 合并 - 金色
                            2017: '#00FF7F', // 双一流 - 绿色
                            2025: '#00CED1'  // 现今 - 青色
                        };
                        return specialYears[year] || null;
                    })()
                });
            }
        }
        
        function project3D(lx, ly, lz, rotX, rotY) {
            let x = lx * Math.cos(rotY) - lz * Math.sin(rotY);
            let z = lx * Math.sin(rotY) + lz * Math.cos(rotY);
            let y = ly;
            let y2 = y * Math.cos(rotX) - z * Math.sin(rotX);
            let z2 = y * Math.sin(rotX) + z * Math.cos(rotX);
            const perspective = 1200;
            const scale = perspective / (perspective + z2);
            return { x: centerX + x * scale, y: centerY + y2 * scale * 0.6, scale, z: z2 };
        }
        
        function drawClearSphere(x, y, radius, color, opacity, glow = false) {
            const r = radius;
            
            // 发光效果（可选）
            if (glow) {
                const glowGradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(x, y, r * 0.5, x, y, r * 2);
                glowGradient.addColorStop(0, color + '40');
                glowGradient.addColorStop(1, color + '00');
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.arc(x, y, r * 2, 0, Math.PI * 2);
                ctx.fillStyle = glowGradient;
                ctx.globalAlpha = opacity * 0.5;
                ctx.fill();
                ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
            }
            
            const gradient = ctx.createRadialGradient(
                x - r * 0.3, y - r * 0.3, r * 0.1,
                x, y, r
            );
            gradient.addColorStop(0, '#ffffff');
            gradient.addColorStop(0.2, color);
            gradient.addColorStop(0.8, color);
            gradient.addColorStop(1, adjustBrightness(color, -40));
            
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(x, y, r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.fillStyle = gradient;
            ctx.globalAlpha = opacity;
            ctx.fill();
            ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
            
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.arc(x, y, r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.strokeStyle = adjustBrightness(color, -20);
            ctx.lineWidth = 1;
            ctx.globalAlpha = opacity * 0.8;
            ctx.stroke();
            ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
            
            return r;
        }
        
        function adjustBrightness(hex, amount) {
            const num = parseInt(hex.slice(1), 16);
            const r = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, (num >> 16) + amount));
            const g = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, ((num >> 8) & 0x00FF) + amount));
            const b = Math.max(0, Math.min(255, (num & 0x0000FF) + amount));
            return '#' + (r << 16 | g << 8 | b).toString(16).padStart(6, '0');
        }
        
        function drawSpiral() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
            
            spiralNodes.forEach(node => {
                const proj = project3D(node.localX, node.localY, node.localZ, 0, rotationY);
                node.x = proj.x; node.y = proj.y; node.scale = proj.scale; node.z = proj.z;
            });
            
            const baseRadius = Math.min(width, height) * 0.18;
            
            ctx.beginPath();
            const pathPoints = [];
            for (let i = 0; i <= totalYears; i += 0.2) {
                const progress = i / totalYears;
                const angle = progress * rings * Math.PI * 2;
                const proj = project3D(
                    Math.cos(angle) * baseRadius,
                    (1 - progress) * spiralHeight - spiralHeight / 2,
                    Math.sin(angle) * baseRadius, 0, rotationY
                );
                pathPoints.push(proj);
            }
            
            for (let i = 1; i < pathPoints.length; i++) {
                const avgZ = (pathPoints[i-1].z + pathPoints[i].z) / 2;
                const opacity = Math.max(0.15, Math.min(0.5, (1 - avgZ / 600) * 0.5));
                
                ctx.beginPath();
                ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(96, 165, 250, ${opacity})`;
                ctx.lineWidth = 2.5 * Math.min(pathPoints[i-1].scale, pathPoints[i].scale);
                ctx.moveTo(pathPoints[i-1].x, pathPoints[i-1].y);
                ctx.lineTo(pathPoints[i].x, pathPoints[i].y);
                ctx.stroke();
            }
            
            const sortedNodes = [...spiralNodes].sort((a, b) => b.z - a.z);
            
            sortedNodes.forEach(node => {
                const size = node.size * node.scale;
                const opacity = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(1, (1 - node.z / 600)));
                // 使用特殊颜色或渐变色
                let color;
                if (node.specialColor) {
                    color = node.specialColor;
                } else {
                    const hue = 200 + ((node.year - startYear) / totalYears) * 60;
                    color = `hsl(${hue}, 70%, 60%)`;
                }
                
                // 特殊年份发光效果
                const shouldGlow = node.specialColor && [1956, 2001, 2017, 2025].includes(node.year);
                drawClearSphere(node.x, node.y, size, color, opacity, shouldGlow);
                
                const keyEvent = keyEvents.find(e => e.year === node.year);
                if (keyEvent) {
                    ctx.font = `bold ${9 * node.scale}px PingFang SC`;
                    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
                    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
                    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
                    ctx.fillText(node.year, node.x, node.y);
                    
                    ctx.font = `${8 * node.scale}px PingFang SC`;
                    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${opacity * 0.95})`;
                    ctx.textAlign = 'left';
                    ctx.fillText(keyEvent.label, node.x + size + 4, node.y - 6);
                    ctx.font = `${7 * node.scale}px PingFang SC`;
                    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${opacity * 0.7})`;
                    ctx.fillText(keyEvent.desc, node.x + size + 4, node.y + 6);
                } else if (node.year % 10 === 0) {
                    ctx.font = `${9 * node.scale}px PingFang SC`;
                    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${opacity * 0.85})`;
                    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
                    ctx.fillText(node.year, node.x, node.y - size - 5);
                }
            });
        }
        
        function drawSolarSystem() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, width, height);
            
            animationTime += 0.016; // 动画时间
            
            const orbitRadiusY = Math.min(width, height) * 0.35 * zoomLevel;
            const orbitRadiusX = Math.min(width, height) * 0.22 * zoomLevel;
            // collegeNodes = [];  // 已移除：避免时序竞争
            
            let renderObjects = [];
            
            // 中心太阳 - 带脉动效果
            const pulseScale = 1 + Math.sin(animationTime * 2) * 0.05;
            renderObjects.push({
                type: 'sun',
                lx: 0, ly: 0, lz: 0,
                radius: 20 * pulseScale,
                color: '#3b82f6'
            });
            
            // 22个学院
            colleges.forEach((college, i) => {
                const angle = (i / colleges.length) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2;
                const lx = Math.cos(angle) * orbitRadiusX;
                const ly = Math.sin(angle) * orbitRadiusY;
                const lz = 0;
                
                renderObjects.push({
                    type: 'college',
                    index: i,
                    lx, ly, lz,
                    radius: 14,
                    color: college.color,
                    name: college.name
                });
                
                // 专业围绕学院旋转
                if (college.majors && college.majors.length > 0) {
                    // 初始化旋转角度
                    if (majorRotationAngles[i] === undefined) {
                        majorRotationAngles[i] = Math.random() * Math.PI * 2;
                    }
                    
                    // 专业旋转动画
                    majorRotationAngles[i] += 0.008 + i * 0.001; // 不同学院旋转速度略有不同
                    
                    const majorOrbitRadius = 50 * zoomLevel;
                    college.majors.forEach((major, j) => {
                        const majorAngle = majorRotationAngles[i] + (j / college.majors.length) * Math.PI * 2;
                        
                        // 椭圆轨道 + 垂直波动
                        const mlx = lx + Math.cos(majorAngle) * majorOrbitRadius;
                        const mly = ly + Math.sin(majorAngle) * majorOrbitRadius * 0.4;
                        const mlz = Math.sin(majorAngle * 2) * 20 + Math.cos(animationTime * 3 + j) * 10;
                        
                        renderObjects.push({
                            type: 'major',
                            parentIndex: i,
                            lx: mlx, ly: mly, lz: mlz,
                            radius: 4,
                            color: college.color,
                            majorData: major,
                            collegeName: college.name,
                            angle: majorAngle
                        });
                    });
                }
            });
            
            renderObjects.forEach(obj => {
                const proj = project3D(obj.lx, obj.ly, obj.lz, solarRotX, solarRotY);
                obj.x = proj.x; obj.y = proj.y; obj.scale = proj.scale; obj.z = proj.z;
            });
            
            renderObjects.sort((a, b) => b.z - a.z);
            
            // 绘制轨道环（装饰效果）
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.ellipse(centerX, centerY, orbitRadiusX * 0.8, orbitRadiusY * 0.8, 0, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(96, 165, 250, 0.1)';
            ctx.lineWidth = 1;
            ctx.stroke();
            
            // 连接线 - 带动画效果
            const majors = renderObjects.filter(o => o.type === 'major');
            majors.forEach(major => {
                const parent = renderObjects.find(o => o.type === 'college' && o.index === major.parentIndex);
                if (parent) {
                    const opacity = Math.max(0.2, Math.min(0.6, (1 - major.z / 600) * 0.6));
                    
                    // 渐变连接线
                    const gradient = ctx.createLinearGradient(parent.x, parent.y, major.x, major.y);
                    gradient.addColorStop(0, major.color + Math.round(opacity * 255 * 0.8).toString(16).padStart(2, '0'));
                    gradient.addColorStop(1, major.color + Math.round(opacity * 255 * 0.3).toString(16).padStart(2, '0'));
                    
                    ctx.beginPath();
                    ctx.moveTo(parent.x, parent.y);
                    ctx.lineTo(major.x, major.y);
                    ctx.strokeStyle = gradient;
                    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
                    ctx.stroke();
                }
            });
            
            // 绘制球体
            renderObjects.forEach(obj => {
                const opacity = Math.max(0.6, Math.min(1, (1 - obj.z / 600)));
                
                if (obj.type === 'major') {
                    // 专业球 - 带拖尾效果
                    const tailLength = 3;
                    for (let t = tailLength; t >= 0; t--) {
                        const tailOpacity = opacity * (1 - t / tailLength) * 0.3;
                        const tailAngle = obj.angle - t * 0.15;
                        const college = colleges[obj.parentIndex];
                        const tailRadius = 50 * zoomLevel;
                        const angle = (obj.parentIndex / colleges.length) * Math.PI * 2 - Math.PI / 2;
                        const clx = Math.cos(angle) * orbitRadiusX;
                        const cly = Math.sin(angle) * orbitRadiusY;
                        
                        const tx = clx + Math.cos(tailAngle) * tailRadius;
                        const ty = cly + Math.sin(tailAngle) * tailRadius * 0.4;
                        const tz = Math.sin(tailAngle * 2) * 20;
                        
                        const tailProj = project3D(tx, ty, tz, solarRotX, solarRotY);
                        
                        ctx.beginPath();
                        ctx.arc(tailProj.x, tailProj.y, obj.radius * tailProj.scale * (1 - t / tailLength * 0.5), 0, Math.PI * 2);
                        ctx.fillStyle = obj.color;
                        ctx.globalAlpha = tailOpacity;
                        ctx.fill();
                        ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
                    }
                }
                
                const r = drawClearSphere(obj.x, obj.y, obj.radius * obj.scale, obj.color, opacity, obj.type === 'sun');
                obj.screenRadius = r;
                
                if (obj.type === 'sun') {
                    ctx.font = 'bold 13px PingFang SC';
                    ctx.fillStyle = '#fff';
                    ctx.textAlign = 'center';
                    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
                    ctx.fillText(selectedYear, obj.x, obj.y);
                    
                } else if (obj.type === 'college') {
                    // 重要：r就是screenRadius，必须显式存储
                    collegeNodes.push({ 
                        x: obj.x, 
                        y: obj.y, 
                        screenRadius: r,  // 使用绘制后的实际屏幕半径
                        collegeIndex: obj.index,
                        name: obj.name,
                        color: obj.color
                    });
                    if (obj.index < 3) console.log(`[填充] 学院${obj.index}: ${obj.name}, 位置(${obj.x.toFixed(0)}, ${obj.y.toFixed(0)})`);
                    
                    ctx.font = `bold ${8 * obj.scale}px PingFang SC`;
                    ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,255,255,${opacity * 0.9})`;
                    ctx.textAlign = 'left';
                    ctx.textBaseline = 'middle';
                    const displayName = obj.name.length > 6 ? obj.name.substring(0, 6) : obj.name;
                    ctx.fillText(displayName, obj.x + r + 5, obj.y);
                }
            });
        }
        
        function animate() {
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                if (autoRotate && !isDragging) rotationY += 0.003;
                drawSpiral();
            } else {
                drawSolarSystem();
            }
            requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }
        
        function zoomIn() {
            zoomLevel = Math.min(2.5, zoomLevel + 0.3);
        }
        
        function zoomOut() {
            zoomLevel = Math.max(0.5, zoomLevel - 0.3);
        }
        
        let lastSolarClickTime = 0;
        let lastSolarClickedNode = null;
        
        function checkSolarClick(x, y) {
            if (currentView !== 'solar') return;
            
            const currentTime = Date.now();
            
            for (const node of collegeNodes) {
                const dist = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - node.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - node.y, 2));
                if (dist < node.screenRadius + 35) {
                    if (lastSolarClickedNode === node && currentTime - lastSolarClickTime < 500) {
                        showCollegeModal(node.collegeIndex);
                        lastSolarClickTime = 0;
                        lastSolarClickedNode = null;
                    } else {
                        lastSolarClickTime = currentTime;
                        lastSolarClickedNode = node;
                    }
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        
        function showCollegeModal(collegeIndex) {
            const college = colleges[collegeIndex];
            document.getElementById('collegeName').textContent = college.name;
            document.getElementById('collegeName').style.color = college.color;
            document.getElementById('majorCount').textContent = (college.majors ? college.majors.length : 0) + '个专业';
            
            const majorList = document.getElementById('majorList');
            majorList.innerHTML = '';
            
            if (college.majors && college.majors.length > 0) {
                college.majors.forEach(major => {
                    const item = document.createElement('div');
                    item.className = 'major-item';
                    item.innerHTML = `<div class="major-name">${major.name}</div><div class="major-hint">点击查看详情</div>`;
                    item.onclick = () => showMajorDetail(major, college.name, college.color);
                    majorList.appendChild(item);
                });
            } else {
                majorList.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;color:rgba(255,255,255,0.4);padding:20px;font-size:12px;">暂无本科专业</div>';
            }
            
            overlay.classList.add('show');
            collegeModal.classList.add('show');
        }
        
        function closeCollegeModal() {
            collegeModal.classList.remove('show');
            overlay.classList.remove('show');
        }
        
        function showMajorDetail(major, collegeName, color) {
            closeCollegeModal();
            
            document.getElementById('majorDetailTitle').textContent = major.name;
            document.getElementById('majorDetailTitle').style.color = color;
            
            document.getElementById('majorDetailCode').textContent = major.code || "无";
            document.getElementById('majorDetailDuration').textContent = major.degree || "无";
            document.getElementById('majorDetailDegree').textContent = major.degree || "无";
            
            // 显示原所在院系和归属学院
            document.getElementById('majorDetailOriginalDept').textContent = major.original_dept || major.original_college || "无";
            document.getElementById('majorDetailCollege').textContent = major.college || collegeName;
            
            majorDetail.classList.add('show');
        }
        
        function closeMajorDetail() {
            majorDetail.classList.remove('show');
            overlay.classList.add('show');
            collegeModal.classList.add('show');
        }
        
        overlay.addEventListener('click', () => {
            closeCollegeModal();
            closeMajorDetail();
        });
        
        let lastClickTime = 0;
        let lastClickedNode = null;
        let clickTimeout = null;
        
        function checkClick(x, y) {
            if (currentView !== 'spiral') return;
            
            const currentTime = Date.now();
            const sortedNodes = [...spiralNodes].sort((a, b) => a.z - b.z);
            
            for (const node of sortedNodes) {
                const dist = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - node.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - node.y, 2));
                if (dist < node.size * node.scale + 15) {
                    // 双击检测
                    if (lastClickedNode === node && currentTime - lastClickTime < 500) {
                        clearTimeout(clickTimeout);
                        showSolarSystemWithTransition(node.year);
                        lastClickTime = 0;
                        lastClickedNode = null;
                    } else {
                        lastClickTime = currentTime;
                        lastClickedNode = node;
                        showYearPopup(node);
                    }
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
        
        function showYearPopup(node) {
            const keyEvent = keyEvents.find(e => e.year === node.year);
            tooltip.querySelector('.year').textContent = node.year + '年';
            tooltip.querySelector('.count').textContent = '专业: ' + node.count + '个';
            tooltip.querySelector('.event').textContent = keyEvent ? keyEvent.label + '：' + keyEvent.desc : '';
            
            let left = node.x + 20;
            let top = node.y - 80;
            if (left + 180 > width) left = node.x - 200;
            if (top < 80) top = node.y + 20;
            
            tooltip.style.left = left + 'px';
            tooltip.style.top = top + 'px';
            tooltip.classList.add('show');
            
            clearTimeout(clickTimeout);
            clickTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                tooltip.classList.remove('show');
            }, 3000);
        }
        
        function showSolarSystemWithTransition(year) {
            const transitionOverlay = document.createElement('div');
            transitionOverlay.style.cssText = `
                position: fixed;
                top: 0;
                left: 0;
                right: 0;
                bottom: 0;
                background: radial-gradient(circle at center, rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.3) 0%, rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.9) 100%);
                z-index: 500;
                display: flex;
                flex-direction: column;
                align-items: center;
                justify-content: center;
                opacity: 0;
                transition: opacity 0.4s ease-in-out;
            `;
            
            transitionOverlay.innerHTML = `
                <div style="font-size: 48px; font-weight: bold; color: #60a5fa; margin-bottom: 20px;">
                    ${year}
                </div>
                <div style="font-size: 16px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.7); margin-bottom: 30px;">
                    ${getMajorCount(year)}个专业
                </div>
                <div style="font-size: 14px; color: rgba(255,255,255,0.5);">
                    正在加载学院数据...
                </div>
            `;
            
            document.body.appendChild(transitionOverlay);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                transitionOverlay.style.opacity = '1';
            }, 50);
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                showSolarSystem(year);
                transitionOverlay.style.opacity = '0';
                setTimeout(() => {
                    transitionOverlay.remove();
                }, 400);
            }, 800);
        }
        
        function showSolarSystem(year) {
            selectedYear = year;
            currentView = 'solar';
            solarRotX = 0.5;
            solarRotY = 0;
            zoomLevel = 1;
            majorRotationAngles = []; // 重置旋转角度
            backBtn.classList.add('show');
            hint.classList.add('hidden');
            hintSolar.classList.add('show');
            zoomControls.classList.add('show');
        }
        
        function showSpiral() {
            currentView = 'spiral';
            selectedYear = null;
            backBtn.classList.remove('show');
            hint.classList.remove('hidden');
            hintSolar.classList.remove('show');
            zoomControls.classList.remove('show');
            closeCollegeModal();
            closeMajorDetail();
        }
        
        function showTooltip(x, y, node) {
            const keyEvent = keyEvents.find(e => e.year === node.year);
            tooltip.querySelector('.year').textContent = node.year + '年';
            tooltip.querySelector('.count').textContent = '专业: ' + node.count + '个';
            tooltip.querySelector('.event').textContent = keyEvent ? keyEvent.label + '：' + keyEvent.desc : '';
            let left = x + 12, top = y - 60;
            if (left + 180 > width) left = x - 195;
            if (top < 80) top = y + 15;
            tooltip.style.left = left + 'px';
            tooltip.style.top = top + 'px';
            tooltip.classList.add('show');
        }
        
        function hideTooltip() { tooltip.classList.remove('show'); }
        
        canvas.addEventListener('wheel', (e) => {
            if (currentView === 'solar') {
                e.preventDefault();
                if (e.deltaY < 0) {
                    zoomIn();
                } else {
                    zoomOut();
                }
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                isDragging = true;
                autoRotate = false;
                lastTouchX = e.clientX;
            } else {
                solarDragging = true;
                solarLastX = e.clientX;
                solarLastY = e.clientY;
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                if (isDragging) {
                    rotationY += (e.clientX - lastTouchX) * 0.005;
                    lastTouchX = e.clientX;
                } else {
                    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
                    const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
                    const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
                    let found = false;
                    const sortedNodes = [...spiralNodes].sort((a, b) => a.z - b.z);
                    for (const node of sortedNodes) {
                        if (Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - node.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - node.y, 2)) < node.size * node.scale + 15) {
                            showTooltip(e.clientX, e.clientY, node);
                            canvas.style.cursor = 'pointer';
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    if (!found) { hideTooltip(); canvas.style.cursor = 'grab'; }
                }
            } else {
                if (solarDragging) {
                    solarRotY += (e.clientX - solarLastX) * 0.006;
                    solarRotX += (e.clientY - solarLastY) * 0.004;
                    solarRotX = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1.4, solarRotX));
                    solarLastX = e.clientX;
                    solarLastY = e.clientY;
                }
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('mouseup', () => { isDragging = false; solarDragging = false; });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
            const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
            const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
            
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                checkClick(x, y);
            } else {
                checkSolarClick(x, y);
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => { isDragging = false; solarDragging = false; hideTooltip(); });
        
        let initialPinchDistance = 0;
        let initialZoomLevel = 1;
        
        canvas.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                isDragging = true;
                autoRotate = false;
                lastTouchX = e.touches[0].clientX;
            } else {
                if (e.touches.length === 2) {
                    initialPinchDistance = Math.hypot(
                        e.touches[0].clientX - e.touches[1].clientX,
                        e.touches[0].clientY - e.touches[1].clientY
                    );
                    initialZoomLevel = zoomLevel;
                } else {
                    solarDragging = true;
                    solarLastX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                    solarLastY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                }
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (currentView === 'spiral' && isDragging && e.touches.length === 1) {
                rotationY += (e.touches[0].clientX - lastTouchX) * 0.005;
                lastTouchX = e.touches[0].clientX;
            } else if (currentView === 'solar') {
                    console.log(`[双击] 学院页面，collegeNodes数量: ${collegeNodes.length}`);
                if (e.touches.length === 2) {
                    const currentDistance = Math.hypot(
                        e.touches[0].clientX - e.touches[1].clientX,
                        e.touches[0].clientY - e.touches[1].clientY
                    );
                    zoomLevel = Math.max(0.5, Math.min(2.5, initialZoomLevel * (currentDistance / initialPinchDistance)));
                } else if (solarDragging && e.touches.length === 1) {
                    solarRotY += (e.touches[0].clientX - solarLastX) * 0.006;
                    solarRotX += (e.touches[0].clientY - solarLastY) * 0.004;
                    solarRotX = Math.max(0.1, Math.min(1.4, solarRotX));
                    solarLastX = e.touches[0].clientX;
                    solarLastY = e.touches[0].clientY;
                }
            }
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('touchend', (e) => {
            const touch = e.changedTouches[0];
            const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
            const x = touch.clientX - rect.left;
            const y = touch.clientY - rect.top;
            
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                if (Math.abs(touch.clientX - lastTouchX) < 10) {
                    checkClick(x, y);
                }
            } else {
                if (e.touches.length === 0 && Math.abs(touch.clientX - solarLastX) < 10) {
                    checkSolarClick(x, y);
                }
            }
            isDragging = false;
            solarDragging = false;
        });
        
        canvas.addEventListener('dblclick', (e) => {
            const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
            const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
            const y = e.clientY - rect.top;
            
            if (currentView === 'spiral') {
                const sortedNodes = [...spiralNodes].sort((a, b) => a.z - b.z);
                for (const node of sortedNodes) {
                    const dist = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - node.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - node.y, 2));
                    if (dist < node.size * node.scale + 15) {
                        showSolarSystemWithTransition(node.year);
                        return;
                    }
                }
            } else if (currentView === 'solar') {
                for (const node of collegeNodes) {
                    const dist = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(x - node.x, 2) + Math.pow(y - node.y, 2));
                    if (dist < node.screenRadius + 35) {
                        showCollegeModal(node.collegeIndex);
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }
        });
        
        backBtn.addEventListener('click', showSpiral);
        
        resize();
        window.addEventListener('resize', resize);
        animate();
    </script>
</body>
</html>
